<script>
    var $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents = {};

    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

        $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents = {

            facebookPixel: null,
            customEvent: false,
            pixelFired: false,
            events: {
                EPrice: {
                    name: "EPrice",
                    type: "click",
                    value: ".results_table .primary-cta .button-form, #details-page-ctabox .maincta-row .button-form, .cta-box .vdp-primary.button-form, #cta-mobile-button"
                },
                                DILeads: {
                    name: "DILeads",
                    type: "advanced",
                    value: "none"
                },
                                SRP: { // Old SRP / VRP
                    name: "SRP",
                    type: "element",
                    value: $(".page-vehicle-results-page")
                },
                LSRP: { // Lightning SRP/VRP
                    name: "LSRP",
                    type: "element",
                    value: $(".page-template-page-lightning")
                },
                VDP: {
                    name: "VDP",
                    type: "element",
                    value: $(".page-vehicle-display-page")
                },
                Lead: {
                    name: "Lead",
                    type: "url",
                    value: "thank-you"
                },
                Parts: {
                    name: "Parts",
                    type: "url",
                    value: "parts"
                },
                Service: {
                    name: "Service",
                    type: "url",
                    value:"service"
                }
            },
            init: function() {
                this.checkCustomEvents();
            },

            checkCustomEvents: function() {
                var self = this;
                for(eventName in self.events) {
                    if(!self.customEvent) {
                        switch(self.events[eventName].type) {
                            case "element":
                                if(
                                    typeof self.events[eventName].value !== "undefined"
                                    &&
                                    self.events[eventName].value.length > 0
                                )
                                    self.customEvent = eventName;
                                break;
                            case "advanced":
                                self.advancedLeadTracking()
                                break;
                            case "url":
                                var url = location.href;
                                var searchString = new RegExp(self.events[eventName].value, "g");
                                if(url.search(searchString) !== -1)
                                    self.customEvent = eventName;
                                break;
                            case "click":
                                var clickEvent = eventName;
                                $("body").on('click', self.events[eventName].value, {name: self.events[eventName].name}, self.fireClickEvent);
                                break;
                        }
                    }
                }

                self.fireFacebookEvents();
            },

            advancedLeadTracking: function() {
                jQuery(document).bind('di_event', function(e, data) {
                    let eventData = {}
                    
                    // console.log("EVENT", data)

                    // set up consistent data that is sent regardless of event type
                    eventData.visit_id = data.visit_id
                    eventData.visitor_id = data.visitor_id

                    // attach data based on event type/name
                    switch (data.name) {
                        case "chat":
                            eventData.type = "chat"
                            eventData.label = data.label
                            eventData.chatName = data.custom_data.provider.name
                            eventData.name = data.custom_data.provider.firstName + " " + data.custom_data.provider.lastName
                            console.log("FB tracking Conversations", eventData)
                            fbq('trackCustom', "Chat", eventData)
                            break
                        case "form_submit":
                            eventData.type = "form_submit"
                            eventData.form_name = data.custom_data.form.name
                            eventData.form_type = data.custom_data.lead.entry.type
                            console.log("FB tracking Form Submit", eventData)
                            fbq('trackCustom', "FormSubmit", eventData)
                            break
                        case "click":
                            if (data.label === "Call") {
                                eventData.type = "click_to_call"
                                eventData.department = data.custom_data.call.department
                                console.log("FB tracking Click To Call", eventData)
                                fbq('trackCustom', "ClickToCall", eventData)
                            }
                            break
                    }
                });
            },

            fireClickEvent: function(e) {
                let customData = {};
                                customData.leadTriggerClasses = $(e.currentTarget).attr('class');
                customData.leadTriggerText = $(e.target).text();
                console.log(e.target, "The above element was clicked, which sends this FB Remarketing Event: '" + e.data.name + "'");
                fbq('trackCustom', e.data.name, customData);
            },

            fireFacebookEvents: function() {

                var self = this;

                // Enqueue the `fbevents.js` script
                self.facebookPixels = ["561509911121372"];
                !function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s)
                {if(f.fbq)return;n=f.fbq=function(){n.callMethod?
                n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};
                if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
                n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
                t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
                s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window, document,'script',
                'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');

                // Create the `fqb` event
                for(pixel in self.facebookPixels) {
                    fbq('dataProcessingOptions', []);
                    fbq('init', self.facebookPixels[pixel]);
                }

                // Handle any found custom events
                if(self.customEvent) {
                    console.log("FB Remarketing Event: '" + self.customEvent + "'");
                                        if(self.customEvent == "VDP" && typeof inventory_localization == "object") {
                        var customData = inventory_localization.vehicle;
                        console.log(customData);
                        fbq('trackCustom', self.customEvent, customData);
                        
                    } else {
                                            fbq('trackCustom', self.customEvent);
                        var vins = [];
                        $('.vehicle-wrap').each(function (i, el) {
                            vins.push($(this).find('div[data-vin]').data('vin'));
                        });
                        if(vins.length === 0){
                            $('.vehicle-overview').each(function (i, el) {
                                vins.push($(this).attr('id'));
                            });
                        }
                                                                
                        if (self.customEvent == 'LSRP') {
                            document.addEventListener('lightning-vrp-did-change', function(e) {
                                var vins = []

                                $('#lvrp-results-wrapper .result-wrap').each(function(i, el) {
                                    var vehicleVin = $(el).data('vehicle-vin')
                                    vins.push(vehicleVin)
                                })

                                fbq('track', 'Search', {
                                    content_type: 'vehicle', // REQUIRED: DO NOT change this, must be set to 'vehicle'
                                    content_ids: vins,
                                });
                            });
                        } else {
                            fbq('track', 'Search', {
                                content_type: 'vehicle', // REQUIRED: DO NOT change this, must be set to 'vehicle'
                                content_ids: vins,
                            });
                        }
                                            
                    }

                                        $(document).ready(function(){
                        jQuery(document).on('savethings-save-vehicle', function(e, data){
                            var info = $(data)[0]['attributes'];
                            var id = info['data-remote-id']. value;
                            var make = info['data-make']. value;
                            var model = info['data-model']. value;
                            var year = info['data-year']. value;
                            fbq('track', 'AddToWishlist', {
                            content_type: 'vehicle', // REQUIRED: DO NOT change this, must be set to 'vehicle'
                                content_ids: [id],
                                make: make,
                                model: model,
                                year: year,
                                currency: 'USD'
                            });
                        });
                    });
                                        self.pixelFired = true;

                }
                // Send the pageview
                fbq('track', 'PageView');
            }
        };

        $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents.init();
    });

</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

            //**************************************************
            //  Open Overlay for All Overlays
            //**************************************************

            /*
                What it does:

                When we click on "open-overlay", we open the overlay and show it.
                If overlay is open, then we hide all toolOverlays & show the overlay we want.
                If user clicked on a close button over the same trigger twice, we close the overlay and hide all toolOverlays
            */
            var showFullOverlayDisplay = false;
            var openOverlay = $('.open-overlay');
            var toolOverlays = $('.toolOverlay');
            var closeAllOverlays = $('.close-overlay, .mobile-tabs .mobile-tab .mobile-tab-label');

            // close overlay when we click on an active icon or when we click on closeAllOverlays targets
            function closeOverlay() {
                // if item has class of active - we are trying to close the overlay and hide all toolOverlays
                $('#fullOverlay').removeClass("open");
                // revert body to correct styles
                $('body').css('overflow-y', 'initial');
                // hide all toolOverlays
                toolOverlays.hide();
                // set showFullOverlayDisplay to false
                showFullOverlayDisplay = false;
            }

            // when close button or mobile tabs are clicked on we want to close overlay & reset everything.
            closeAllOverlays.click(function() {
                // close overlays
                closeOverlay();

                //reset all icons
                $('.icon-toggle-js').removeClass('active');
            });


            // When we click on '.open-overlay' -
            openOverlay.click(function() {
                var openOverlayTrigger = $(this);

                // we check if the trigger we clicked on is already 'active'
                if (openOverlayTrigger.hasClass('active')) {
                    closeOverlay();
                } else {
                    // if we are clicking on a openOverlayTrigger for the first time we are checking if the overlay is already open.
                    if (showFullOverlayDisplay) {
                        // if overlay is already open - we want to hide all toolOverlays and show the toolOverlay we want
                        toolOverlays.hide().removeClass('showTarget');
                        $('#' + openOverlayTrigger.attr('target') + "__overlay").show().addClass("showTarget");
                    } else {
                        // Set  showFullOverlayDisplay to true
                        showFullOverlayDisplay = true;
                        // show fullOverlay
                        $('#fullOverlay').addClass("open");
                        // set overflow on body to hidden to prevent page from moving when scrolling within overlay
                        $('body').css('overflow-y', 'hidden');
                        //show target based on trigger
                        $('#' + openOverlayTrigger.attr('target') + "__overlay").show().addClass("showTarget");
                    }
                }
            }); // end of openOverlay functions


            //**************************************************
            //  Mobile Menu JS
            //**************************************************

            /*
                What it does:

                On "devices > main menu," when we tap on a parent
                top level item, we will grab the sub-menu of that
                item, clone it, and paste it into an overlay. Users
                can only dive down one level deep. CSS is hiding
                the 3rd level for now!
            */

            // runs when orientation changes - when ipad pro goes from portriat to landscape or vice versa
            window.addEventListener('orientationchange', mobileJS);

            function mobileJS() {
                var submenuparent = $('.menu-item-has-children a.dropdown-toggle');
                var submenuoverlay = $('#menu-submenu-overlay');
                var mobile_menu = $('ul[id^="menu-main-menu"].nav');

                $('#back-button').on('click tap', function() {
                    submenuoverlay.removeClass('active');
                    submenuoverlay.find('.menu-wrapper .dropdown-menu').remove();
                    mobile_menu.removeClass('hide-item');
                });

                submenuparent.on('click tap', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var that = $(this);

                    // grabbing title to set in the overlay
                    var title = that.attr('title');

                    // if Title Attribute isn't populated in Wordpress, use anchor text
                    if (title === undefined) {
                        title = that.text();
                    }

                    // we are cloning the sub-menu attached to the parent link we clicked on - we add the "nav" class for css styles
                    var submenu = that.siblings('ul.dropdown-menu').clone().addClass('nav');
                    submenuoverlay.scrollTop = 0;

                    // set heading to the overlay
                    $('#heading-title span').html(title);

                    mobile_menu.addClass('hide-item');

                    // append the new sub-menu to the overlay
                    submenuoverlay.find('.menu-wrapper').append(submenu);
                    submenuoverlay.addClass('active');

                    // this runs inside this function because the menu-submenu-overlay doesn't exist until it's cloned and populates
                    var subsubmenu = $('#menu-submenu-overlay .dropdown-menu.nav li.menu-item-has-children > a');

                    var subsubmenu_dropdownmenus = $('#menu-submenu-overlay .dropdown-menu.nav li.menu-item-has-children ul.dropdown-menu');

                    subsubmenu.on('click tap', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();

                        if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
                            $(this).removeClass('active');
                            $(this).siblings('ul.dropdown-menu').removeClass('active');
                        } else {
                            subsubmenu_dropdownmenus.removeClass('active');
                            subsubmenu.removeClass('active');
                            $(this).addClass('active');
                            $(this).siblings('ul.dropdown-menu').addClass('active');
                        }
                    })

                });
            }

            if ($(window).width() < 1025) {
                mobileJS();
            };
        });
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
            //**************************************************
            //  Device Icon Toggle
            //**************************************************

            /*
                What it does:

                When a "icon-toggle-js" is clicked, we are
                toggling an active class on this item, and the CSS
                will toggle what is shown (default icon / close icon)
            */

            var toggleButtons = $('.icon-toggle-js');

            toggleButtons.on('click tap', function() {

                if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
                    $(this).toggleClass('active');
                } else {
                    toggleButtons.removeClass('active');
                    $(this).addClass('active');
                }
            });

            //**************************************************
            //  Megamenu Fix for iPad Pro
            //**************************************************

            /*
                What it does:

                On iPad Pro, when a user taps on a desktop menu item, that menu item click event is turned off, and we are showing the submenu.
            */

            var isiPad = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;

            // runs when orientation changes - when ipad pro goes from portriat to landscape or vice versa
            window.addEventListener('orientationchange', adjustMenu);

            function adjustMenu() {
                var menuItems = $('#header .nav .menu-item.menu-item-has-children > a');

                menuItems.on('click tap', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    closeMenu();
                    $(this).next().addClass('show');
                    return false;
                });

                $(document.body).click(function() {
                    closeMenu();
                });

                var closeMenu = function() {
                    menuItems.next().removeClass('show');
                }
            }

            if (isiPad && $(window).width() > 1025) {
                // Runs on page load
                adjustMenu();
            };

        });
    </script>
